msg:That was the second time I had stayed at this hotel purely due to its magnificence. I booked a deluxe room and it was perfectly furnished with wood that gave it a scent of retro style unlike many modern and hi-tech hotels. And the lobby of the hotel is another thing worth coming for, it is a pure pleasure and lustre, everything is made down to the smallest detail.
The only thing that I was disappointed in was a lack of decent sauna and hammam. There was a sauna but it was tiny - just around 1 by 1 square meters and you had to turn it on and wait for it to warm up, and the hammam, which was just as tiny, didn't work at all. The swimming pool was normal, but there was no jacuzzi section (there was a small separate pool that was supposed to be with warm water, but in fact it was quite cool.
Other than that, the breakfast food range was excellent (although not much Western food).
I would definitely recommend this hotel for a one or two day stay.

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Standard Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:11 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted April 8, 2024
msg:Advantages~~
1. Although the hotel was built a few years ago, the hardware is quite good. It can be seen that the design and decoration were extremely attentive. The hotel occupies a large area. When you get off the car, the waiter will immediately welcome you and open the door. The lobby is super grand, clean and bright. It is adjacent to Wuxi International Exhibition Hall and can be reached by subway. There is a large lawn in front of the door. Wuxi Shangxian Lake Wetland Park is separated by a small road. It takes 10 minutes to drive to Sunac Mall. The location is also very good.
2. The room is very large. The bed in the standard room is 1.35 meters wide. There is no pressure for families with two children.
The bathroom is also very large. There are seats at the door of the room and rest booths in the corridor. It is very attentive. The quality of the toiletries is very good. The conditioner and body lotion are very easy to use.
3. The breakfast is rich. There are many freshly made Wuxi specialty foods, freshly fried dough sticks and freshly made sesame cakes. The food quality is up to five-star quality.
4. The attitude of the service staff is very good. When checking out, I met the front desk supervisor Zhang Feng who took the initiative to ask about my stay experience. Based on my many years of hotel stay experience, I sincerely put forward some [suggestions] as follows~~
1. The overall style of the hotel is business style But it can be seen that they are trying their best to become a parent-child hotel, but they feel a little powerless. It is recommended to refer to some successful parent-child hotel practices:
1. When checking in, you can take the initiative to send parent-child family gifts (the key chain in Figure 4 was sent after chatting with Zhang Feng, the supervisor, and found out that it was not sent when checking in. This key chain is very delicate and sells for 30 yuan in Sunac Park. The children treated it as a treasure on the way back and were very happy)
2. The children's disposable items can be put into a gift bag and sent out when checking in. I have encountered this in other hotels before. The first impression of staying will be very good
3. The hotel's breakfast restrictions are a bit rigid. My second child is over 1.2 meters, but there is only kindergarten and can't eat anything. However, according to the hotel's breakfast regulations, you need to pay 68 yuan, which is a bit discouraged. It is recommended to consider not only height but also age
4. It is recommended to add some children's meals and tableware for breakfast
Overall, this stay is still very comfortable. The flaws do not cover the merits. I will come to Wuxi every year and will continue to stay with my family in the future. I hope the hotel will attract more parent-child families, especially the advantage of being close to Sunac Park during winter and summer vacations. The business is getting better and better

msg:Worldhotel Grand Juna Wuxi: A cozy home for Suzhou, Wuxi and Changzhou trip
During my just-concluded four-day trip to Suzhou, Wuxi and Changzhou, Worldhotel Grand Juna Wuxi undoubtedly provided me with the most comfortable and unforgettable accommodation experience. From the moment I stepped into the hotel lobby, I was attracted by the elegant and modern design style here.
Meticulous service experience
During my stay, I deeply felt the professionalism and enthusiasm of the hotel staff. Whether it was the reception staff at the front desk or the room service staff, they all showed a high degree of professionalism and meticulous service attitude. Every one of my needs, no matter how big or small, was responded to promptly and thoughtfully.
Comfortable and pleasant guest room environment
The room I stayed in was spacious and bright, and the layout was both warm and elegant. The bed was comfortable and soft, allowing me to enjoy high-quality sleep every night. In addition, the facilities in the room are all available, whether it is the air conditioning temperature, lighting brightness or bathing facilities, they are all very thoughtful, making me feel the comfort of home.
Delicious dining options
The hotel's restaurant also left a deep impression on me. The breakfast is rich in variety, with Chinese and Western food. Whether it is steaming porridge or exquisite and delicious bread and pastries, it makes people's appetite increase. At dinner, I also tried the restaurant's special dishes, and the taste was equally satisfying.
Convenient location
Wuxi Juna Worldhotel is located in the city center, with convenient transportation and many surrounding attractions. Whether it is to go to Wuxi's famous attractions such as Yuantouzhu and Nanchang Street, or to the commercial center for shopping and leisure, it is very convenient.
Summary
In general, Wuxi Juna Worldhotel provided me with an unforgettable accommodation experience. From comfortable rooms, delicious food to warm and thoughtful service, every detail made me feel the hotel's care and professionalism. If I have the opportunity to go to Wuxi in the future, I will definitely choose to stay in this hotel again.
